# kanmind_backend

![Python](https://img.shields.io/badge/-Python-blue?logo=python&logoColor=white)

## рџ“ќ Description

kanmind_backend is a robust and scalable Python-based backend infrastructure designed to power modern task management and productivity applications. Engineered with a focus on security and performance, it provides a comprehensive feature set including a secure RESTful API, seamless database integration, and a sophisticated authentication system to protect user data. To ensure long-term maintainability and developer productivity, the project incorporates a rigorous testing suite and a versatile command-line interface (CLI) for streamlined administrative tasks and rapid backend orchestration.

## вњЁ Features

- рџЊђ Api
- рџ—„пёЏ Database
- рџ”ђ Auth
- рџ§Є Testing
- рџ’» Cli


## рџ› пёЏ Tech Stack

- рџђЌ Python


## рџ“¦ Key Dependencies

```

djangorestframework: 3.16.1
sqlparse: 0.5.5
```

## рџ› пёЏ Development Setup

### Python Setup
1. Install Python (v3.8+ recommended)
2. Create a virtual environment: `python -m venv venv`
3. Activate the environment:
   - Windows: `venv\Scripts\activate`
   - Unix/MacOS: `source venv/bin/activate`
4. Install dependencies: `pip install -r requirements.txt`


## рџ‘Ґ Contributing

Contributions are welcome! Here's how you can help:

1. **Fork** the repository
2. **Clone** your fork: `git clone https://github.com/NicolausFeldtmann/kanmind_backend.git`
3. **Create** a new branch: `git checkout -b feature/your-feature`
4. **Commit** your changes: `git commit -am 'Add some feature'`
5. **Push** to your branch: `git push origin feature/your-feature`
6. **Open** a pull request

Please ensure your code follows the project's style guidelines and includes tests where applicable.
